Important News

October Report on Innovation Work of the Ministry of Education This Year (2)

(8) Promulgation, Interpretation, and Review of Educational Laws and Regulations

(1) Issued a circular to implement the Executive Yuan's order to amend Articles 2, 7, and 10 of the Organizational Outline of the Municipal and County Literature Committees, requiring notification; (2) Submitted a report to the Executive Yuan in response to an order to prepare steps for the National Compilation and Translation Bureau; requesting review and approval; (3) Instructed the National Central University to interpret the regulations for military training of transfer students, requiring notification; (4) Approved Li Wenwei's request to interpret the ambiguity of "equivalent level" mentioned in Article 17 of the Provisional Regulations for Secondary Schools, issuing an approval notice; (5) Instructed the Shandong Provincial Department of Education to interpret the qualifications of graduates from the special and regular departments of the First Provincial Rural Normal School, requiring transfer and notification; (6) Instructed the Shandong Provincial Department of Education that commendation for private donations of books should be handled in accordance with Article 8 of the Regulations for Commending Donations for Educational Undertakings, requiring transfer and notification; (7) Telegraphed the Hunan Provincial Department of Education that, according to an order from the Executive Yuan, whether women can apply for educational rent grains from their maternal clan after marriage should be determined by the clan's regulations, requiring transfer and notification; (8) Approved twenty-one single regulations from various provinces and cities: Regulations of the Hubei Provincial Public Science Experiment Hall Purchasing Committee; Organizational Regulations of County Education Bureaus in Henan Province; General Rules for Soviet Staff Children's Schools and Foreign Schools in the Eastern Province Special District; Regulations on the Employment of Soviet Educational Personnel Affiliated with the Eastern Province Special District Department of Education; Foreign Teacher Registration Regulations of the Eastern Province Special District; Rules of the Foreign Teacher Registration Committee of the Eastern Province Special District Department of Education; Rules for the Eastern Province Special District Department of Education Governing Various Meetings Held by Soviet Staff Children's Schools and Foreign Schools; General Rules for Summer Game Fields of Foreign Schools in the Eastern Province Special District; General Rules for Summer Resorts for Students of Soviet Staff Children's Schools in the Eastern Province Special District; Articles of Association for Research Groups on Teaching Methods in Soviet Staff Children's Schools in the Eastern Province Special District; Regulations for Foreign Schools in the Eastern Province Special District; General Rules for Parent-Teacher Associations in Foreign Schools in the Eastern Province Special District; Competition Regulations for Students of All Levels of Schools in Chahar Province; Revised Rules of Procedure for the School Affairs Conference of the National Zhejiang University; Detailed Rules for Inspectors of the Education Department of the Anhui Provincial Government; Revised Organizational Outline of the Shandong Provincial Education Funding Audit Committee; Revised Regulations of the Shandong County Education Funding Committee; Revised Accounting Regulations for County and Municipal Schools at All Levels and Educational Institutions in Shandong Province; Revised Accounting Regulations for County Education Bureaus in Shandong Province; Provisional Measures for the Assumption of Office and Handover of Responsible Personnel in Directly Subordinate Institutions of the Fujian Provincial Department of Education; Measures for Rewarding Writings by the Henan Provincial Department of Education.

(9) Commendations for Donations to Education

(1) Submitted a report to the Executive Yuan based on a report from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education regarding Kuang Qiyong's donation of over 240,000 yuan for educational undertakings, specifically requesting review and approval to be forwarded to the National Government for an explicit commendation; (2) Issued three first-class awards, two second-class awards, and four third-class awards for donations to education.

(10) Review and Approval of Textbooks

(1) Approved for review and approval: *Physics Student Experiment Course for Senior High Schools*; *New Junior Geometry for Middle Schools*; (2) Approved for publication: *World Children's Literature Series: Lubo's Big Dream*; *National Tales: Magpie Forest*; *Flower Shovel*; *Ape Island*; *Selling Bean Boy*; *New Physics*; *Middle School Mineralogy Textbook*; *Kindergarten New Songs*; *Rainbow Feather Robe*; *Song Performance*; *77 Sweet Songs for Elementary School Students*; *Intermediate Poultry Science*; *Practical East Asian Reader*.

Solicitation of Academic Awards by the Fujian Education Department

Total Prize Money: 1,000 Yuan

The Fujian Provincial Department of Education, in order to promote academic pursuits, has specially collaborated with the Department of Finance, the Department of Construction, the Department of Civil Affairs, and the Security Office to jointly raise 1,000 yuan for academic awards. The first solicitation of essays will be held on December 31st. The methods are as follows: (1) This award will solicit essays on one topic, divided into two sessions. Each session will solicit essays on two topics, and the best entry for each topic will be selected: 1st place: 50 yuan; 2nd place: 30 yuan; 3rd place: 20 yuan. However, if there are no outstanding entries, it is better to leave the position vacant than to fill it with a substandard work. The number of selected entries may be reduced in part or in whole as appropriate. (2) The topics for the essay contest will be determined by the agencies that contribute to the award money. (3) The essay contest will be judged by experts invited by each agency contributing to the award money. (4) All people from all walks of life in this province who have deep research or concrete and effective plans regarding the essay topics are welcome to participate. (5) Each person may submit essays on multiple topics, but only one essay per topic is allowed. (6) The writing style is not limited, but essays should be over 3,000 words in length. The names, chapters, and pages of all books and newspapers referenced should be noted in the essay or listed at the end. Applicants may issue a request to the essay solicitation agency to borrow reference materials. (7) Essays must be written clearly and punctuated. The author's name, place of origin, age, brief resume, place of service or school attended, and a seal must be included at the end. (8) The first submission of essays must be mailed by registered post to the Department of Education by December 31st of the 20th year of the Republic (1931), with the words "Essay Contest" clearly marked on the envelope. (9) The names and rankings of the selected entries for the first essay contest will be announced in the Fujian Republic Daily on January 20th of the 21st year of the Republic (1932). (10) All selected essays will be published in the Education Department's *Education Weekly* and in the publications of the agencies that contribute to the award money. The topics for the first essay contest are currently being drafted by the Department of Education in consultation with the Department of Finance, the Department of Construction, the Department of Civil Affairs, and the Security Office, and will be officially announced soon.

Local News

Educational Circles Compile a Ten-Year Education Plan

The Shanghai Educational Circles National Salvation United Association has been working extremely hard on national salvation work recently. They believe that the way to save the country should address both the symptoms and the root causes, with education being the foundation. Therefore, at the eleventh executive committee meeting the other day, they decided to compile a ten-year education plan as a standard for future training. They have separately appointed educators to compile it. The research methods are as follows:

A. Scope of the Plan: Schools at all levels and mass education. B. Appointed Experts to Plan: 1. Elementary Education Plan: Zhao Lüqing, Li Bojun, Qian Xuanqing, Chen Pingyi, Xu Zihua, Hu Shuyi, Sheng Zhensheng, Sheng Langxi, and Gu Yinqian are appointed to draft the plan, convened by Zhao Lüqing. 2. Secondary Education: (1) General Secondary School Plan: Shu Xincheng, Zheng Xigu, Ge Zulan, Liao Maoru, Ni Wenya, Lu Buqing, and Wang Xiaoying are appointed to draft the plan, convened by Ni Wenya. (2) Normal Education Plan: Jiang Wenyu, Shao Shuangqiu, Shen Yizhen, Ren Mengxian, and Wang Maozu are appointed to draft the plan, convened by Jiang Wenyu. (3) Vocational and Supplementary Education Plan: Wang Zhixin, Chen Xuanchan, Huang Renzhi, Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, Pan Yangyao, and Jia Foru are appointed to draft the plan, convened by Yang Weiyu. 3. Higher Education Plan: Ou Yuanhuai, Cao Huiqun, Chu Minyi, Chu Fucheng, He Bingsong, Hu Chunzao, Li Yisheng, Liu Zhanen, and Zhang Yi are appointed to draft the plan, convened by Ou Yuanhuai. 4. Mass Education Plan: Lei Binnan, Meng Xiancheng, Ma Zongrong, Gao Jiansi, Shang Zhongyi, and Yu Qingtang are appointed to draft the plan, convened by Gao Jiansi. C. Deadline for Submission: The end of December this year. All types of plans should be submitted to the association, which will collect them and appoint a review committee to review them. D. Submit to the Ministry of Education for Review and Implementation: This entire plan will be submitted to the Ministry of Education for review and implementation after being reviewed by the association.

Anti-Japanese Federation of University Students

│Held the First Eleventh Representative Assembly│

Initiated and Convened a Shanghai Municipal Citizens' Assembly

Requested Anti-Japanese Associations from All Circles to Allocate Funds

Held a General Review of the Youth Volunteer Army

According to the resolution of the 23rd executive committee meeting of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of University Students in this city, the 11th representative assembly was held at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Corps to discuss all urgent issues. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

Representatives from Guanghua University, Wenhua College, Shanghai Art College, Daxia University, Jiangnan College, Fudan University, Tongde Medical College, Chinese Medicine College, Datong University, Aurora University, Jiaotong University, Zhengfeng College of Arts, Hujiang University, Chinese Medical College, Dongya Physical Education College, Sino-French Engineering College, Merchant Marine School, Shanghai Law School, Soochow Law School, Jinan Chinese Public School, College of Political Science and Law, and Southeast Medical College attended.

Details of the Meeting: Nie Haihang of Zhonggong chaired the meeting; Lu Xizhen of Fudan served as the recorder. After the formal opening ceremony, the director of the General Affairs Department of Daxia reported on the association's economic situation; (2) The director of the Military Training Department of Jinan reported on the regional review situation; (3) The director of the Propaganda Department of Zhonggong reported on the difficulties in the work due to lack of funds; (4) The representative attending the National Student Association in Nanjing reported on the attendance process; (5) The Jiaotong University representative reported on continuing to participate in the association's anti-Japanese work. After the reports, the discussion began.

Matters for Discussion: (1) The executive committee submitted a proposal to hold a unified anti-Japanese rally of all students against the violent Japanese, but it had missed the timing and lacked funding, so it was proposed to stop it and ask the representative assembly to ratify it. Resolution: ratified. (2) The executive committee submitted a letter to Ning and Yue representatives, but it had missed the timing, so it was proposed to stop sending it and ask the representative assembly to ratify it. Resolution: ratified. (3) The director of the Propaganda Department of Zhonggong proposed that the General Affairs Department allocate 300 yuan within three days to facilitate propaganda work. Resolution: The representative assembly will first resolve the entire financial method of the association before allocating propaganda funds. (4) The association requested that all anti-Japanese associations allocate 2,000 yuan per month from the national salvation fund for anti-Japanese expenses, to be handled by the executive committee. Resolution: passed. (5) The citizens' assembly will be carried out by the executive committee, and the date will be determined by the association in conjunction with all anti-Japanese associations. Resolution: passed. (6) The association should oppose the auction of confiscated Japanese goods by all anti-Japanese associations. Resolution: passed and handed over to the executive committee for handling. (7) Suggestions to the citizens' assembly: (A) Telegraph the Chairman of the National Government to order his subordinates to strictly guard the territory; (B) Telegraph the National Government to severely punish the officials responsible for the failure of the Tianjin Incident. Resolution: passed. (8) Hold a general review of the volunteer army of university students. The funding, time, and location will be handled by the executive committee. Resolution: passed.

University Anti-Japanese Associations Appeal for Displaced Students from the Northeast

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of University Students, considering that most of the students from the Northeast have been displaced and have nowhere to turn since the Japanese invasion of Shenyang, yesterday specially petitioned the government to provide relief as soon as possible, and telegraphed all schools across the country to find ways to accommodate them. The original text is recorded below:

A Petition to the National Government for Relief for Displaced Students from the Northeast: Since the violent Japanese soldiers invaded the Northeast, they have committed all kinds of atrocities, including rape, looting, and robbery. They are especially wary of cultural groups and educational institutions, causing much destruction by shelling schools and shooting students, resulting in hundreds of thousands of students in the Northeast being displaced. This not only wastes their studies but also harms the foundation of the country and goes against the principles of the government to encourage young people to study and save the country. Now, students from the Northeast are wandering around aimlessly. Although they have the heart to study, they have nowhere to go. They feel uneasy and cannot even talk about saving the country. If this continues, the future is worrying. Therefore, we have prepared a petition, hoping that you will review and approve it, and quickly accommodate and resettle the displaced young students from the Northeast to maintain the foundation of the country and plan for national affairs. The youth of the Northeast will be fortunate, and the future of the country will be fortunate. Respectfully presented to Chiang, Chairman of the National Government.

A Telegram to All Schools and Newspapers Across the Country, Forwarded to All Educational Institutions and Schools Across the Country: Since the violent Japanese occupied the Northeast, they have arbitrarily destroyed and worked hard to undermine cultural groups and educational institutions, shooting, shelling, and doing everything possible, causing students in the Northeast to be displaced. This not only wastes their studies but also harms the foundation of the country and goes against the original intention of the government to encourage young people to study and save the country. Considering this, our association dares to earnestly request that you find ways to accommodate them as soon as possible so that students in the Northeast will not suffer from the discontinuation of learning and the wandering of displacement. Our education will be fortunate, and the country will be fortunate. We respectfully telegram you.

University Student Anti-Japanese Association Telegrams Requesting the Expulsion of Japanese Troops

(National News Agency) The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of University Students in this city, considering that the violent Japanese invaded Liaoning and Jilin, not only did not abide by the resolution of the League of Nations to withdraw troops by a deadline, but have recently intensified their efforts to invade Heilongjiang Province and disturb Tianjin, and if the Japanese troops do not withdraw after the deadline, troops will be dispatched to expel them from the country immediately. The telegram is recorded as follows: To the National Government of Nanjing: The fall of Liaoning and Jilin has angered the entire country. Our country, in order to maintain world peace, appealed to the League of Nations, hoping for fair arbitration. Therefore, the League of Nations had a resolution on November 16 that the Japanese troops must completely withdraw, which was announced to the world. Now that the time is pressing, the violent Japanese not only stated that they would never withdraw their troops, but also expanded their atrocities, attacking Heilongjiang Province and attacking Tianjin, and are actively plotting to disturb other important cities in our country and advocating joint management of China, deceiving the great powers. Their malicious intentions are outrageous. They despise the righteous advice of the League of Nations and undermine the credibility of the League of Nations. If our country is still an autonomous country, we should use iron blood and pledge to make a final struggle with perseverance. At that time, if the violent Japanese do not withdraw their troops, we respectfully ask the government to quickly send troops to drive the barbarians out of the country, defend our territory, wash away our humiliation, save China from sinking, and boost the prestige of China. The national crisis is imminent, and we are deeply saddened. (The rest is omitted.)

Details of the League of Nations Educational Observation Group's Inspection in Shanghai

Dr. Pei Liang and Dr. Lang Jifan, members of the League of Nations Educational Observation Group, accompanied by Inspector Wang Shenming of the Ministry of Education, visited Zhejiang. Two members of the group arrived in Shanghai on the 8th and transferred to Beijing by train that night. Dr. Pei and Dr. Lang Jifan were accompanied by the section chiefs assigned by the Municipal Education Bureau, who took turns to visit Tongji University, Jiaotong University, the Academia Sinica, Social Sciences, Geology, Physics, Chemistry, and Engineering Research Institutes on the morning of the 9th. That evening, the Municipal Education Bureau hosted a banquet for the group members at Xinghualou, inviting Inspector Wang of the Ministry of Education, principals of major primary and secondary schools in the city, deans of various colleges, and section chiefs and inspectors of the Education Bureau to attend. During the banquet, Chinese education issues were discussed. On the 10th, they visited Shanghai Provincial Middle School and Zhonghua Vocational School. On the morning of the 11th, they visited the Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School and Xicheng Primary School. In the afternoon, they visited the Municipal Education Bureau to observe educational administration and discuss Shanghai's educational issues. On the morning of the 12th, accompanied by Inspector Wang of the Ministry of Education, they took a train to Wuxi and other places to visit.

Vocational Education Society Investigates National Vocational Education

Soliciting Plans for Promoting Vocational Education

Yesterday, the Chinese Vocational Education Society sent letters to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, soliciting plans for promoting vocational education, reports, and lists of vocational schools. The original letter stated: Our society is dedicated to researching and promoting vocational education. Since the recent Japanese invasion of the Northeast, in order to fundamentally save the country, we feel more strongly the need to cultivate practical talents and increase production capacity. Our society has first enlisted experts to form a Vocational Education Promotion Design Committee, which, on the one hand, seeks future plans for vocational education from various places and investigates the current situation of vocational education in various places, and on the other hand, waits for the authorities in various places to raise questions and indicate to our society to carefully discuss and answer from both academic theory and facts for adoption. At the same time, the essentials will be publicly announced in the *Education and Vocational* monthly magazine for public viewing. We have long appreciated your bureau's enthusiasm for vocational education. In this time of national crisis, we would like to promote and implement it with greater efforts. We humbly request you to grant us the following three documents: 1. Your office's plans for promoting vocational education, or the entire education plan including the plan for promoting vocational education. 2. Your office's report on the current status of vocational education, or the entire report on the education situation including the report on the current status of vocational education. 3. A list of vocational schools in your office, as well as the names, subjects, addresses, and lists of educational institutions of a vocational education nature. We earnestly request that you quickly check and send them to us. We are deeply grateful. If there are any questions about vocational education that need to be studied, please feel free to inform our society, and our colleagues will do their best to provide answers. Our society has been publishing the *Education and Vocational* monthly magazine for fifteen years without interruption, and it has now been issued to the 130th issue. If your office has not yet read it, we will be happy to present it to you upon request, in order to seek great teaching.

Municipal Circulating Library Opens

The circulating library established by the Municipal Education Bureau of this city on the second floor of the City God Temple has gradually increased to more than 5,000 visitors per day since it opened last year. Because the library is narrow and insufficient, the library specifically asked the Municipal Education Bureau to borrow a room from the Yimiao Board of Directors. Later, it stopped opening from the 2nd of this month to add embellishments to the original library. It has been completed on the 11th and will be open for reading as usual on the 13th. Except for Mondays, it is open daily from 8:00 AM to 5:00 PM. There are now two reading rooms in the library, and all kinds of books, magazines, and newspapers are displayed on the shelves, and readers can browse at will. All kinds of books can be freely borrowed outside the library for reading without any handling fees or restrictions on the number of times. A brief introduction will be sent immediately upon request.

Dongya Physical Education College Sports Meet Held in the Rain

Those Who Won First Place in the Municipal Games Are Not Allowed to Participate

The Dongya Physical Education College in Lujiawan in this city was scheduled to hold a sports meet on the previous two days, as reported in this newspaper. Unexpectedly, the weather was not good, and it rained during the period. The school decided not to postpone it in order to train the students' physical fitness. Except for the field events, which could not be held due to excessive water accumulation on the field, the track events were still held. It rained all day, and there were very few guests. Male and female athletes each showed their bravery and competed bravely regardless of the rain. Their clothes were soaked, but they were not afraid and did not lose interest because no one was watching. After the reporter arrived at the scene, they did not see the two girls, Zhang Pingxian and Qian Xingsu, who won the first and second place in the overall score in the city's sports meet, which was quite strange. After inquiring, it was learned that in order to popularize and increase the interest of the second-class players, anyone who won first place in more than one sport in the city's sports meet was generally not allowed to participate. The results of the competition are recorded below:

Men's Group

100 Meters: Peng Guangxin, Dong Keyou, Dan Zhaorong, Yu Zhirui, 12 seconds

200 Meters: Lu Jingguang, Yu Zhirui, Dan Zhaorong, Dong Keyou, 24.8 seconds

400 Meters: Peng Xuemo, Miao Zhishan, Pei Langu, Li Feiran, 56 seconds

800 Meters: Zhang Dianxi, Miao Zhishan, Tan Xi, Lü Mingcheng, 2:20.4

1500 Meters: Zhang Dianxi, Lü Mingcheng, Hou Dechong, Liu Yongchang, 5:02.6

10000 Meters: Tan Xi, Huang Zizhen, Zhou Shujun, Ouyang Yingxue, 41:40.4

110-Meter Hurdles: Yuan Hanmin, Wei Rongtao, Lu Jialin, Bai Zhaosheng, 19.4 seconds

400-Meter Low Hurdles: Tang Zuozhou, Li Cunfu, Peng Guangxin, Xie Zhaosheng, 63 seconds

Women's Group

50 Meters: Lu Puzhen, Sheng Bi, Zheng Lixing, Zhang Shuxin, 7.4 seconds, breaking the school record

100 Meters: Liu Jingfang, Lu Puzhen, Ao Tianyun, Liu Baoshu, 13.8 seconds, tying the national record

200 Meters: Xia Fenlü, Mou Yuxrui, Ao Tianyun, Zhang Mingxia, 34 seconds

80-Meter Hurdles: Liu Jingfang, 16 seconds, tying the North China record

As the competition was about to end, Ms. Liu Jingfang requested to perform the 200 meters. The chief referee approved, and five or six people including Lu Puzhen accompanied her. Four watches were used to time. Ms. Liu was first, with a score of 28.8 seconds. Second was Lu Puzhen, with a score of 32.4 seconds. The results were excellent.

Local News

All Circles Should Rise Up and Substantially Assist Heilongjiang Province

Sending Telegrams of Condolences Is Not as Good as Providing Military Funds and Sending Aid

Since Ma Zhanshan, the Acting Chairman of Heilongjiang Province, adopted legitimate defense and repelled the Japanese invaders, all circles have been greatly encouraged and have sent telegrams of condolences. However, empty words, although enough to inspire morale, will not be a long-term solution without substantial assistance, considering the small number of hungry and tired national troops facing the rampant Japanese flames. Yesterday's proposals by Wang, Wu, Zou, and Wang deserve the deep attention of all Shanghai citizens and compatriots across the country.

Telegram from Peace Conference Representatives Wang, Wu, and Zou

Yesterday's Telegram to the Six Representatives of the Nanjing Peace Conference

Please Forward to Those in Charge the Idea of Legitimate Defense

Wang Jingwei, Wu Chaochu, and Zou Lu, the Guangdong representatives remaining in Shanghai for the peace and unification conference, jointly telegraphed yesterday to Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Zhang Jingjiang, Li Shizeng, Chen Mingshu, and Wu Tiecheng, the six representatives of the Nanjing peace conference, requesting them to forward the message to those in charge, urging them to quickly reinforce Ma Zhanshan. The original telegram is recorded below:

"To Representatives Cai Jiemin, Zhang Puquan, Zhang Jingjiang, Li Shizeng, Chen Zhenru, and Wu Tiecheng of Nanjing: Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of Heilongjiang, clearly upholds the meaning of defending the territory and fulfills the responsibility of safeguarding it. Compared to those who hold military power but abandon territory and those who do not resist foreign invasion, the difference is like heaven and earth. Recent reports indicate that Japan is increasing its troops to invade Heilongjiang, and Chairman Ma's situation is extremely dangerous. We request that you forward the message to those in charge to quickly send reinforcements, so as not to let patriotic and virtuous men be trapped in desperate situations. At the peace conference, the Guangdong representatives stated in the context of diplomatic unification that they could not agree with the policy of not resisting foreign invasion. The gentlemen also agreed that when foreigners invade our territory and we resist, international law recognizes this as legitimate defense, which is an absolutely legal action. We request that you quickly forward this and implement it, and please reply. Wang Zhaoming, Wu Chaochu, Zou Lu."

Conversation with Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce

We Should Do Our Best to Raise Funds to Assist

Do Not Let Heilongjiang Province Become the Second Tainan

Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stated that the Heilongjiang army is fighting bravely against the Japanese for the country, establishing extraordinary merits, and all sectors should urgently raise funds to help them, so as not to fail due to exhaustion of funds and lack of assistance. Yesterday, he issued a statement to the Xin Sheng News Agency, saying, "The Heilongjiang army has been confronting the violent Japanese at Nenjiang since the fourth day of the month, and it has been nearly ten days. The Japanese are increasing their troops and transporting weapons day by day, plotting a major offensive. Although the soldiers of that province are trying their best to support and fight hard, that province is the poorest of the three provinces. Recently, since the Tao'ang Road was blocked, the transportation of goods jointly operated by Bei'ning has been interrupted, commerce has been depressed, and income has decreased. Moreover, the Guangxin Official Silver Bank, on which the province relied for its funds, has had all its cash taken away by Wanguo Bin, so the shortage of military funds is almost certain. The soldiers of that province are fighting hard while enduring hunger, striving for the dignity of our nation. We, the people who are fortunate enough to be outside the battlefield, have not heard of any rescue efforts besides empty words of comfort. How can we face the soldiers who are dying in the front? The business community in Harbin has already raised 2 million to assist military funds. Overseas Chinese in the Philippines have also reportedly discussed raising funds to assist. This city seems unable to remain indifferent. We must remember the defense of Tainan by Liu Yanting in the year of Yiwu, which also failed due to exhaustion of funds and lack of assistance. The difficult and arduous situation is detailed in Yao Xiguang's "Eastern Military Records." In order to support Ma's righteous act of prioritizing territorial defense, we must not stand by and watch the fire from across the river, and let Heilongjiang Province become the second Tainan of that day. We should immediately unite and do our best to raise funds to assist, in order to solidify the morale of the army in that province, and let future generations know what to learn from."

Important Telegram from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of the Five Southeastern Provinces

Telegraph Request to Vice Zhang, Yan, and Feng to Quickly Dispatch Large Troops to Reinforce

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of the Five Southeastern Provinces sent two telegrams yesterday:

(1) Telegram to Ma, the Acting Chairman of Heilongjiang Province: "General Ma Zhanshan, under your command, after a long and silent night, we suddenly heard of your victory at Nenjiang, which revitalized the hearts of dying people. We have received telegrams every day, learning that the enemy is retaliating on a large scale, and our army is in a bitter battle. Looking north to the dark clouds, our hearts are filled with worry. The lives of the entire nation now depend on you. If you waver, it would be unbearable to imagine. We implore you to overcome danger as if walking on flat ground, and to die rather than leave, as a lesson to those soldiers who do not know how to defend against aggression, and to further deter the enemy. Our country's army has courage and knows the right direction, and is fully capable of fighting a battle, but it is only because the commanding generals are cowardly and willing to retreat, which leads to disaster. Our association, feeling the emptiness of the League of Nations meetings and the unfulfilled ambitions of the violent Japanese, telegraphed Vice Commander-in-Chief Zhang as early as last month, bitterly stating the righteousness of defending the territory and avenging the enemy, urging him to risk his life and leave the customs immediately to command the various armies and calmly respond to the battle, and also requesting that Generals Bai and Huan come out of retirement and unite against the enemy. Now we telegraph again, requesting that you quickly dispatch large troops to reinforce, so as not to let the general bear the brunt alone. We hereby telegraph our best wishes to the general, may China live forever, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of the Five Southeastern Provinces."

Zhang Ji and Chen Mingshu Arrived in Shanghai on Orders to Visit Wang

Wang Requested that the Central Government Quickly Study the General Amnesty Case

The Reform of the Political System Case Should Be Approved by the Fourth Plenary Session

The Conflict of the Two Parties' Proposals Has Been Resolved with Remedial Measures

Zhang Ji and Chen Mingshu, the Beijing representatives to the Beijing-Guangdong Peace Unification Conference, came to Shanghai on a special express train yesterday morning at about 8:00 a.m. on orders to discuss the telegrams issued by the Guangdong side when the Fourth National Congress of the Kuomintang was held. After getting off the train, they visited Wang Jingwei, the Guangdong representative, at his residence in the French Concession at about 9:00 a.m. and talked for about an hour. In addition to representing the central government and requesting the Guangdong side to issue a unified telegram in accordance with the general intention of the telegram issued by the Beijing side when the Fourth National Congress was held, they also reported the situation of the meeting held by the Beijing side's Fourth Plenary Session the day before, and expressed President Chiang's sincere attitude towards peaceful unification. Wang agreed to telegraph the Guangdong side according to their intention, and asked Chen and others to return to Beijing and quickly urge the central government to study the political amnesty case, so that all comrades of our country's party can unite as soon as possible to meet the expectations of the people. After Zhang and Chen left, a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency specially visited Wang for an interview. According to Wang, (1) Regarding the content of the meeting between Chen Zhenru and others in Shanghai, it is as described by the reporter above. (2) According to the fourth item of the proposal passed by the last meeting of the Peace Preparatory Committee, namely, "The first plenary meeting of the fourth session shall amend the Organic Law of the National Government and reorganize the government," this case, on the surface, seems to overturn the political system reform plan passed by the Preparatory Committee, and is instead decided by the first meeting of the fourth session. However, according to Wang, the one passed by the Preparatory Committee will be passed in the future, and then submitted by both parties for ratification when the Fourth Plenary Session discusses the proposal, which is equivalent to the one decided by the Preparatory Committee being approved by the Fourth Plenary Session in general. Therefore, there is no reason to overturn anything that has been passed by the previous Preparatory Committee. (3) Regarding the conflict of proposals in the Fourth Plenary Session of both parties, such as one case that the Beijing side can pass but the Guangdong side cannot pass, or the Guangdong side can pass but the Beijing side cannot pass, Wang said that this is inevitable in fact, but both parties have formulated a method, namely, the second item agreed upon at the last meeting of the Peace Preparatory Committee: "All proposals of the Fourth Plenary Session of both parties shall be handled by the Fourth Central Executive Committee at its first meeting in Nanjing."

The Finance and Economic Committees Will Hold Regular Meetings in Beijing

Song Ziwen Made a Speech Yesterday

The Guomin News Agency said that regarding the establishment of a Finance Committee by the National Government, Finance Minister Song made a speech, saying that the establishment of a Finance Committee that can represent all sectors of the country is a new era in our country's financial community. Since then, the budget can be established, and the income and expenditure of the national treasury can be made public. For four years, this ministry has repeatedly proposed the necessity of establishing a budget for the government, but due to various problems, it has not been realized until recently, when the country is in great difficulty, and the government and the people know that this move can no longer be delayed. In the two provinces of Hubei and Jiangxi, the red disaster is overwhelming, in the north there is the rebellion of Shi Yousan, in the south there is the change in Guangdong Province, the Yangtze River basin is suffering from floods, the world economy is in chaos and depression, and our country's business situation is also in a desperate situation. Recently, the violent Japanese invasion has occupied our eastern provinces. In the past half year, the disasters and pains suffered by our country are unprecedented in other countries. Even one of them is enough to subvert a general government. However, the National Government has gone through thousands of difficulties and dangers, and has not yet been shaken. Its perseverance is really commendable. Moreover, the series of events in the past few months has made the people of the whole country know that at this time of national crisis, various problems must be dealt with in a practical manner, and they can no longer be perfunctory. The Finance Committee is also the Ningxin'er in this period of national crisis. The purpose of establishing this conference is also in line with the opinions exchanged between representatives of Beijing and Shanghai and the banking community. Among the organizational outline, the following points are most noteworthy: (1) In addition to important military and political personnel from the government, there are also representatives from the industrial, commercial and academic circles in the organization of the committee, and the national finance can be studied openly by all parties in the country. (2) Several vacancies in the committee are reserved for recommendation by Guangdong. (3) All military and political expenses must be reviewed by the committee. (4) All income and expenditure of the government shall be announced every two weeks. (5) The issuance of public bonds must also be audited by the committee. The central government does not want to meet Guangdong with weapons, and the Guangdong side does not want to meet the central government with weapons. The people of the country have also unanimously hated all internal wars. It is the consensus of the people of the country that they have been tired of chaos for a long time. In the future, this will surely be achieved. There is no need to use divination. It is also expected that military expenditure can be gradually reduced. The committee is now scheduled to hold its first meeting in Nanjing this Sunday to discuss the major plans for national finance. It is also noteworthy that when the Finance Committee holds its meeting, the National Economic Committee will also hold its first meeting in Nanjing on the same day. The organization of the Economic Committee is the same as that of the Finance Committee. In addition to government personnel, there are leaders from industrial, commercial, financial, and educational circles. The purpose of the conference is to express itself to the world in a regular and systematic way, and to develop China with the help of the League of Nations. The League of Nations has sent an educational investigation team to China, and its team investigating our country's water conservancy and road construction projects has also embarked on its journey. I deeply hope that after the establishment of the Finance Committee and the Economic Committee, on the one hand, the government's economic needs can be met with systematic economic methods, and on the other hand, the domestic industrial, commercial, and transportation industries can be developed at the same time. I sincerely wish the two conferences a bright future."

Opening of the Shanghai County Agricultural Product Exhibition

The Shanghai County Farmers' Education Hall, in order to promote agricultural products and improve farmers' income, held the opening ceremony of the Agricultural Product Exhibition at 1:00 p.m. on the 12th of this month. Attendees included Yang Peiwen, representative of the Ministry of Education, Shou Biao, representative of the Ministry of Industry, Shi She, representative of the Provincial Government, Wang Huazhao, representative of the Department of Finance, Lu Feizhi, representative of the Department of Agriculture and Mines, Lu Youchang of the Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office, Yan Shenyu, County Governor, Peng Liren, Lv Zhe, and Jiang Yanchou of the County Party Department, Zhang Yisan, representative of the Construction Bureau, and more than 1,000 farmers. The meeting was chaired by Yan Shenyu, President, Cai Youchang recorded, and the prayer was performed as usual. The President's report briefly stated that today's opening of the first Shanghai County Agricultural Product Exhibition has been through a long period of preparation and many aspects of help, and it was established today. Although it is raining, the attendance is still enthusiastic. The purpose of our opening this meeting is because Shanghai County is close to the urban area, and farmers are running to the urban area. Everyone is unwilling to farm, which leads to a daily decline in agricultural income and increasing difficulties in farmers' livelihoods. We want to use the results of this competition exhibition to make everyone interested in agriculture and gradually improve agricultural work. We want everyone to know the importance of agriculture and pay attention to increasing the production of agricultural products. Moreover, because the Agricultural Education Hall has been running for several years, we want to take an opportunity to show the results and see what the results of the work are. The direction of future progress can be seen at today's venue. There are many products, and there are also many excellent ones. Therefore, I hope that everyone will know that we not only pay attention to the products, but also pay attention to their output. We want everyone to work harder and focus on cultivation, so that the exhibition can progress and develop year by year. This is what we most hope for.

(1) Provincial Representative Shi She's Speech: "The province wants me to represent them in participating in this meeting, which is very gratifying. I have one feeling about the results of this meeting, thinking that the most important thing in our life is food, and China is an agricultural country. The food is not enough every year, and we have to import it from abroad, which makes China poorer year by year and sends a lot of money to foreign countries. To save this loss, we must promote agricultural production and scientific research. Foreign countries pay attention to research, so their output is very high and they can sell it to China. China is such a big country, and we can't even eat enough by ourselves. Isn't it very dangerous? Today's meeting is to ask everyone to find ways to increase agricultural products, improve agriculture, and increase farmers' income. When farmers are rich, the country can also be rich. When the country is rich, China will naturally be strong, and naturally we will not be afraid of Japanese aggression. Therefore, today's agricultural exhibition has a very important definition."

(1) County Party Department Representative Peng Liren's Speech: "There is a problem of poverty in the society now, and everyone feels that there is no food to eat. We want everyone to overcome this difficulty, so we must pay attention to production and promote agriculture. Recently, the situation in Shanghai is mostly difficult to live in, and the countryside is also declining. Farmers are running to Shanghai, and their own farmland is not planted. As a result, they don't see food to eat in Shanghai, and they are still poor. Therefore, the most fundamental and best way to solve the problem of poverty is to promote agricultural production, because agriculture accounts for the main part of the social economy. When production increases, everything can be done. Now the Agricultural Education Hall is opening this exhibition, hoping that everyone will pay attention to increasing agricultural production, which can indirectly solve everyone's problem of eating. I hope everyone will pay more attention and participate more, so that the next conference will be very colorful."

(1) Finance Department Representative Wang Huazhao's Speech: "China is an agricultural country. To seek national wealth and strength, we should pay attention to the improvement of agriculture. China's flood this year required borrowing a large amount of American wheat for relief. If we had accumulated surplus food in normal times, we could have avoided this loss. The meaning of today's meeting is to hope that everyone will do more research in the future, break the old habits, and everyone will have an enterprising spirit. Those who win awards in the agricultural product exhibition competition should be especially happy and strive for further progress. Those who did not win awards should also look at other people's examples and learn other people's methods, so that the next conference can also stand out. That is my greatest hope."

Shanghai City is busy with the canal tax and grain. Measures to Relief Chinese Workers in Japanese Factories

Has been decided by the Anti-Japanese Association after consultation

First Step: Register the Number of Chinese Workers

There are a total of 45 Japanese-owned textile factories in China, with 1,630,430 spindles, 190,844 thread spindles, and 14,082 looms, employing 77,792 Chinese workers. It is estimated that 3,191,769 dan of cotton are used, 823,437 bales of yarn are produced, and 7,587,767 bolts of cloth are produced. Shanghai has the largest number, with 30 factories, 1,148,184 spindles, 189,824 thread spindles, and 9,846 looms. Qingdao is the second largest, followed by Liaoning, Hankou, and Dalian. Since the people of our country automatically cut off economic relations with Japan due to the violent Japanese occupation of our Liaoning and Jilin, Japanese-owned yarn factories in China have become exhausted. The Japanese Textile Industry Association in China has held several meetings to discuss countermeasures. An emergency meeting will be held in Osaka on the 10th to determine fundamental policies, and Chairman Takei Ayazō will be sent to Shanghai to discuss concrete methods. In order to relieve the discharged Chinese workers of Japanese yarn factories, the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association has organized a committee, appointing Lu Jingshi, Fang Jiaobo, Wang Xiaolai, Hou Dachun, Zhang Zilian, and other five people as members. At the same time, it is guiding workers in Japanese yarn factories to organize anti-Japanese associations. The anti-Japanese associations in the eastern and western factories of Shanghai have been formally established. The first step is to start registering the names and numbers of Chinese workers in Japanese yarn factories for record keeping, and the Anti-Japanese Association will consult with leaders of Chinese yarn factories to discuss placement methods. The Central Training Department has also sent personnel to Shanghai to consult with the municipal government and the municipal party department on relief measures. It is reported that concrete relief measures have been determined. When Japanese yarn factories close down, placement can be carried out according to the agreed-upon methods. As for the more than 1,000 workers who voluntarily resigned from the Gongda Yarn Factory, it has been arranged by Lu Jingshi, a member of the Anti-Japanese Association, to be placed in Chinese yarn factories.

Anti-Japanese Association Finds That Zheng Zenan's Bribery Case Was Falsely Accused

Zhu Anqing Should Be Dealt With According to Law for Harbouring Resentment

Ju Jiqiu, a staff member of the secretariat of the Anti-Japanese Association, reported that Zheng Zenan, chairman of the Sugar Industry Association, was bribing to release goods. The 16th Standing Committee meeting previously resolved that the Investigation Department should cooperate with the Economic Isolation Implementation Committee of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to conduct a detailed investigation for verification. Now, according to the Investigation Department's report after clarifying the original case, the 18th Standing Committee meeting resolved: (1) Zheng Zenan was framed by someone harbouring resentment and should be exonerated in the newspaper; (2) Yuan Yu Sugar's bribery to foreigners should be confiscated and not discussed; (3) The Reconnaissance Department should order Zhu Anqing to be handed over to the association for legal action after bail; (4) The anti-bribery staff member Ju Jiqiu should be awarded 200 yuan. The report of the Investigation Department is appended as follows: For the matter of reporting, the entire volume of Zheng Zenan's bribery case was submitted and dispatched, and Comrade Yu Zulun was sent to investigate in detail. Now, according to the reply, after being dispatched, together with Comrade Ye Jiaxing, a member of the Economic Isolation Implementation Committee against Japan, investigated the Zheng Zenan case. After a detailed investigation of all parties involved, the results obtained are summarized responsibly as follows: (1) After the Yuan Yu and Mao He numbers were found by the Sugar Industry Association to be suspected of selling Japanese sugar, the meeting decided on October 4 not to discuss it. Then, after the meeting, Zheng Zenan ordered the two firms to donate 1,500 yuan each as funding for the sugar industry primary school. (2) Zhu Anqing and Zheng Zenan have an old feud, so he instigated Yuan Yu to change the registration to "National Salvation Gold" on the account, and then reported it to the association. (3) When the donation was made, Yu Yizhai, the manager of Yuan Yu, was not in Shanghai. After returning to Shanghai, he talked about it with Zhu Anqing and was fooled by Zhu. After being questioned by colleagues, he urgently wanted to settle the matter and took back the account book. However, Zhu Anqing blackmailed a huge amount of money and lobbied the association staff, and even settled the matter privately. After investigation, Zhu Anqing's first secret report was issued out of personal hatred, and then he wanted to settle the matter, intending to profit from it. This person should be brought to justice to warn against treachery. (4) Zhu Anqing and Zhu Anfu are relatives. The promise of promotion and wealth was initiated by Anfu, and the bribe of 1,000 yuan was handled by Anfu. Now he is avoiding meeting, which is very hateful. (5) Yu Yizhai's inconsistency shows that he is guilty, but judging from the inside story, Yu is indeed a loyal and useless person. This time, he was completely fooled by Zhu Anqing, resulting in a dilemma, and the 1,000 yuan was also taken out by Yu privately. According to this, the investigator believes that the claim is true. Therefore, this report is submitted, hoping for your approval. Respectfully submitted to the Standing Committee.

Prohibit Unscrupulous Merchants from Raising Prices

The Municipal Social Bureau instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: For the matter of compliance, according to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's Instruction Shangzi No. 8562, the Ministry found in February this year that the Fujian National Goods Promotion Association requested the prohibition of raising prices of national goods. The bureau was ordered to issue a sincere announcement. Later, in June, the Executive Yuan issued a letter from the Central Secretariat, and the Hubei Provincial Party Department requested a strict prohibition of unscrupulous merchants from raising prices after the reduction of tariffs. It was re-notified to comply with the record. It is now reported that at this time of vigorously promoting the national goods movement, there are still merchants selling national goods who disregard the overall situation, covet petty profits, and take the opportunity to raise prices for sale, which is extremely hateful. It is important to know that the higher the price of national goods is raised, the smoother the sales of foreign goods will be. It not only infringes on the interests of customers, but also undermines the progress of the group. It is appropriate to reiterate the previous order, that the bureau should transfer to its affiliated chambers of commerce, summon industrialists and merchants to organize a national goods evaluation committee, investigate in detail the national goods sold on the market, and immediately flatten those who raise prices. At the same time, it should announce to the public that if there are unscrupulous merchants raising prices, they are allowed to report them by name and add appropriate punishment to warn and encourage them. This order, for the chamber of commerce to deliberate and reply to.

The Fact That Navy Commander Rear Admiral Carye and His Wife and Daughter Were Rescued by the Asia Empress Wheel Has Been Recorded in Yesterday's Newspaper. It Is Now Learned That the Accident of the Peterfield Was Caused by the Turbulent Current on the Sea Surface of Dongyong Mountain, Which Caused It to Be Washed into a Hidden Reef. The 73 Officers in the Ship Were Also Rescued by the German Company's Passenger Ship Taifunje and Taken to Hong Kong by the Asia Empress. The Two British Warships Sent to Rescue in Hong Kong Are Still There.

Recent Activities of Japanese Residents in Shanghai

Appointed Representatives to Return Home

Entrusted with Important Missions

A Large Number of Japanese Residents Return Home. Since the Anti-Japanese Movement, Japanese Residents in Various Ports along the Yangtze River Have First Sent Their Wives and Children Back to Their Country. Those Who Stayed in Shanghai Are Mostly Men. Recently, the Textile Factories in China Have No Place to Sell Their Goods and Are Gradually Closing Down. Those Japanese Who Work in These Factories and Lose Their Jobs, Together with Their Families, Number About 5,000 People. They Are All Preparing to Depart for Their Country. Industry and Commerce Representatives Return Home. Since Our Country's Economic Isolation from Japan, Japanese Businesses Have Been Greatly Affected. Small Businessmen Feel That Their Daily Lives Are Even More Difficult to Maintain. Since the Disturbances in Tianjin, False Rumors Have Risen in Shanghai. The Shanghai Japanese Chamber of Commerce and Industry Has Held Full Meetings for Several Days. The Social Bureau Ordered Work to Start First

All the Workers of the Shanghai West Xiaoshadu Dahuang Industrial Factory, in View of Japan's Atrocities, Organized Anti-Japanese National Salvation Groups and Implemented Military Training. The Central Government Approves the Membership Registration Rules of the Seamen's Union

The China Seamen's Rectification Committee Ordered Compliance Yesterday

The Membership Registration Rules of the National Seamen's Union Have Been Approved by the Central Training Department's Instruction No. 18080. After Being Ordered, the China Seamen's Union Rectification Committee Instructed Labor Unions All Over the Country to Comply with Them. The Original Text of Its Rules Is Recorded Below. Article 1: The Membership Registration of the Seamen's Union in Various Places Shall Be Handled in Accordance with These Rules. Article 2: In Accordance with the Provisions of Articles 2 and 3 of the Seamen's Union Organization Rules, All Seamen Who Serve in Merchant Ships That Run on Machines and Sail at Sea or on Waters Connected to the Sea, Except for the Following, Shall Be Members of the Seamen's Union and Complete the Registration Procedures: (1) Captain Acting as Captain Grand Second and Third Mates; (2) Chief Engineer Grand Second and Third Engineers; (3) Radio Operators; (4) Doctors; (5) Pilots; (6) Compradors and Business Directors. Article 3: Those with One of the Following Circumstances Shall Not Be Allowed to Perform Registration: (1) The Registrant Has Violated the Three Principles of the People's Comments and Actions and the Investigation Has Concrete Evidence; (2) The Registrant Has Embezzled Public Funds and the Report Has a Basis; (3) The Registrant Has Acts That Endanger the Seamen's Union and the Investigation Has Concrete Evidence. Article 4: Registrants Should Pay Attention to the Following Matters: (1) You Must Personally Fill in the Membership Registration Form When Registering; (2) Anyone Who Has Been a Member of the Seamen's Union Should Bring a Certificate or Equivalent Proof of Documents When Registering; (3) You Must Pay a Registration Fee of Two Angles When Registering. Article 6: If the Registrant Cannot Write, the Registration Staff May Fill in the Registration Form on His Behalf, but He Must Sign or Seal It. Article 7: Registration Staff Should Not Deliberately Make Things Difficult for Seamen's Legal Registration. If There Are Any Cases of Fraudulent Solicitation of Money, the Parties Are Allowed to Report It and Strictly Investigate and Punish It. Article 8: These Rules Shall Be Implemented After Being Resolved by the China Seamen's Union Rectification Committee and Submitted to the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee for Approval.

Donate 10,000 Yuan to Refugees

A Resolution Will Be Submitted at the Annual Meeting of Western Taxpayers in April Next Year to Amend Clause 6 of the Land Regulations. In Addition to the Existing Three Real Estate Committee Members, Two Chinese Can Be Added as Members. At That Time, the Public Concession Bureau Will Express Its Approval. According to the Current Land Regulations North of Yangjingbang, Although There Are No Explicit Provisions Prohibiting Chinese from Serving as Real Estate Committee Members, If You Want to Increase the Number of Members, Legally Speaking, You Must Supplement or Amend the Regulations. According to Many Years of Practice, Amendments Must First Be Resolved by a Special Meeting of Western Taxpayers, and Then Submitted to the Consular Corps for Approval, Then Transferred to the Minister, and Finally Approved by the Chinese Government. However, in Recent Years, It Has Been Extremely Difficult to Obtain the Legal Number of People for a Special Meeting of Western Taxpayers. Therefore, the Board of Directors Decided to Submit It at Next Year's Annual Meeting. Local News Two

The National Government's Flood Relief Association Stipulates Winter and Spring Emergency Relief and Work Relief Measures

The National Government's Flood Relief Committee, in View of the Arrival of Winter and the Urgent Need for Winter Relief, and the Need to Consider Spring Relief Measures at This Time, Has Specially Stipulated Ten Detailed Rules for Winter and Spring Emergency Relief Funds and Food Work Relief Measures. At the Same Time, the Disaster Area Working Group of the Association Also Stipulated Four Winter Relief Guidelines and Three Work Relief Methods for Commissioners in Various Areas, Which Are of Great Importance to the Future of Relieving Victims. Now They Are Recorded as Follows:

The Detailed Rules for Food Work Relief. The Detailed Rules for Winter and Spring Emergency Relief Funds and Food Work Relief Stipulated by the Association Total Ten Articles. Article 1: Within the Number of Relief Funds and Food Allocated to the Disaster-Stricken Counties, They May Be Appropriately Proposed to Subsidize the People to Repair Public Embankments and Implement Work Relief. Article 2: Based on the Amount of Relief Funds and Food That Can Be Used for Work Relief, Verify the Total Number of Projects in the County That Destroyed Public Embankments, and Allocate Them on Average. If There Is No Embankment Disaster County, It Can Be Used to Dig Public Ditches and Build Public Roads, With the Main Purpose of Working in Their Local Area. Article 3: According to the Provisions of Article 2, the Owners of the Embankment and Other Impartial Local People Must Draw Up a Drawing Budget of the Earthwork of the Project and Report It to the Relief Personnel for Review. After Verifying the Earthwork Project of the Whole County, Determine the Subsidiary Composition, and Then Verify That the Landlords in the Embankment Can Complete the Project With the Support of Relief Funds. Otherwise, They Shall Not Be Granted Relief. Article 4: Although the People's Public Embankment Is Assigned to Subsidize Relief Funds and Food, It Must Be Divided into Four Times for Distribution. Distribute It Once When the Work Is 1/4, Distribute It Once When It Is Half, Distribute It Once When It Is 3/4, and Distribute It Once After the Completion and Acceptance. Article 5: If It Is Digging Public Ditches and Building Public Roads, Those Who Can Be Donated by Philanthropists Can Be Incorporated Into the Handling and Work as Much as Possible. Article 6: Whether It Is Repairing People's Public Embankments or Digging Ditches and Building Roads, There Must Be More Than Three Substantial and Credible Local People to Guarantee That They Will Be Responsible for Compensation If the Project Is Not Completed or the Work Is Not Good. Article 7: Whether It Is Subsidizing the Repair of Embankments or Digging Ditches and Building Roads, the Number of Relief Funds That Should Be Given to the Workers Must Be Announced, and It Is Strictly Forbidden for Anyone to Deduct From It. Article 8: The Relief Personnel Must Patrol and Inspect the Work to See Whether It Is in Line With the Original Reported Plan and Whether the Work Is Legal. If There Is Any Discrepancy, They Should Correct It to the Person in Charge. Article 9: Each Time Relief Personnel Distribute Subsidiary Relief Funds or Ditch Road Funds, They Must Supervise How They Are Allocated. Each Time They Issue It, They Must Obtain a Receipt From the Responsible Person and Report It. Article 10: These Detailed Rules Shall Be Reported to the Standing Committee by the Disaster Area Work Organization for Record and Then Promulgated for Implementation.

Winter Relief Implementation Guidelines. At the Same Time, the Disaster Area Working Group of the Association Formulated Four Winter Relief Implementation Guidelines for Commissioners in Various Areas Starting in November: (1) According to the Time Situation, It Should Be the Winter Relief Period. In Addition to the Victims Who Have Not Completely Receded From the Accumulated Water and Cannot Return Home, the Shelters That Have Been Established Should Still Be Relieved. All Areas Where the Water Has Receded Should Be Allowed to Return Home and Prepare to Resume Operations. (2) If There Is a Small Amount of Work Relief That Can Be Handled Locally, Appropriate Amounts Should Be Proposed From the Allocated Emergency Relief Funds and Food and Held Immediately. (Note That the Workplace Under the Jurisdiction of This Group Is Temporarily Focused on Restoring the Main River System's Important Official Embankments. Branches and Embankments, As Well As Roads and Ditches, Etc., Are Difficult to Take Care of for a While. If There Are Such Small Projects That Can Be Carried Out, They Can Be Carried Out Locally Under the Emergency Relief Item. The Emergency Relief Method Is Not Limited to the Two Ends of the Shelter or Providing Food According to the Population. When Possible, Work Relief Is Allowed.) (3) In Areas Where the Water Has Receded, Victims Return Home. Appropriate Travel Expenses or Equivalent Rations Should Be Given According to the Distance of Their Return. Before or Simultaneously, Personnel Should Be Sent to the Countryside to Check Households and Give Tickets in Accordance With the Reporting Rules and Distribute Relief Food. (4) If the Water Has Not Completely Receded From the Entire Territory, the Shelter Should Reduce the Population Returning Home From the Receded Land. If the Water Has Completely Receded, the Shelter Should Be Closed. If There Are Any Helpless Elderly or Weak, They Should Also Be Ordered to Return to Their Hometown to Receive Relief.

Work Relief Work Scope. The Disaster Area Working Group Also Stipulated Three Work Relief Work Scopes: (1) After This Flood, the Official and Civilian Embankments Collapsed and Were Scoured Everywhere. If You Want to Repair Them One by One, It Will Be Difficult to Pad Manpower and Financial Resources. The Work Relief of This Association Should Be Cultivated Separately by Officials and Private Individuals, and the Urgency of Work Should Be Determined and Key Points Should Be Held to Meet the Emergency. (2) Based on This Idea, This Group Should Weigh the Allocation of Grain, Rice, and Funds in Consultation With the Provincial Government and Competent Authorities Where the Project Is Located, Gather Victims, Divide Into Sections for Construction, and Distribute Relief According to the Amount of Work. Local Areas Should Raise Funds to Supplement Relief If It Is Insufficient. (3) It Is Intended That the Work Is Huge and the Funds Are Insufficient, Which Is Inevitable. It Is Intended to Submit a Further Request to the National Government to Raise Relief Funds. If It Is Approved, It Can Reduce the Burden on Local Areas

Delineation of Work Authority. Regarding the Delineation of Work Responsibilities for Work Relief Work, the Disaster Area Working Group Also Stipulated Three Methods: (1) The Various Works Within the Scope of Emergency Relief Are Handled by the Commissioners in Various Areas (Emergency Relief Is Not Limited to Shelters or Food Relief and Money Relief, Etc. When Local Small Projects Can Be Carried Out by Hiring Victims, Those That Can Be Handled by Allocating Funds From Emergency Relief Are Handled by the Commissioners.) (2) Regarding Work Relief and Agricultural Relief Matters, the Commissioners Are Requested to Fully Provide Opinions and Materials in Consultation With Local Officials and Gentry to Develop Implementation Methods by the Work Relief and Agricultural Relief Departments. (3) The Implementation Organization of Work Relief and Agricultural Relief Shall Be Conducted in a Coordinated Manner by the Work Relief Office and the Agricultural Relief Office in Accordance With Local Conditions.

Postal Workers' Union Attention to the You Case

A Document Submitted to the Municipal Party Department and a Letter to the Bar Association

You Bolu, the main culprit in the Baoshan Road tragedy, was tried once by the District Court on the 10th of this month. The official announced that the plaintiff had not arrived, and the trial was rescheduled. It is reported that the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government decided to provide considerable compensation to the family of the deceased. However, after the compensation, all private lawsuits and independent rights of appeal related to the case would be waived by the family. Upon hearing this, the union was deeply suspicious and submitted a request to the Municipal Party Department for clear instructions to resolve their doubts. The union also, because lawyers Zhang Yaozeng and others were willing to defend You, who had slaughtered the people, sent a letter to the Bar Association requesting it to immediately warn Zhang Yaozeng and others to voluntarily terminate their contract to represent You in court and to severely punish the lawyers. The document submitted to the Municipal Party Department and the letter to the Bar Association are recorded below:

To the Municipal Party Department: A Request for Examination and Instructions. You Bolu, while serving as the head of the 5th District of the Public Security Bureau, arbitrarily issued orders and wantonly opened fire, slaughtering patriotic people. His crimes were heinous and aroused public outrage. The families of the dead and wounded had filed public and private lawsuits in court. When the court opened the trial on the 10th of this month, it was heard that the plaintiffs were summoned to your department, so they were unable to attend the court. It was also heard that your department, in conjunction with the municipal government, decided to give considerable compensation to the family of the deceased, but after the compensation, all private lawsuits and independent rights of appeal concerning the case were to be waived by the family. Upon hearing this, we were deeply astonished. The families were innocently victimized, a great tragedy. Even if You were sentenced to the most severe punishment and all of his private property was used for compensation and pensions for the victims, it would still not be enough to redress their grievances. Your department, together with the municipal government, generously provided compensation. It was a sign of compassion and a duty that should be fulfilled. However, the private lawsuits filed in court and the independent rights of appeal, according to the law, how can they be waived? They should continue to be pursued in court to protect legal rights. Our association speaks frankly and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we specifically submit this document to your department for clear instructions to resolve our doubts. We are anxiously awaiting your response.

To the Bar Association: Regarding the report that when the You Bolu case was heard in the District Court on the 10th of this month, lawyers Zhang Yaozeng, Sha Xunyi, and Zhu Shaowen were in court to defend You, we cannot but express our indignation. You Bolu undermined the patriotic movement and slaughtered patriotic people. His atrocities are unforgivable. All who have conscience should hate him. Your association has always upheld justice, demonstrated the law, and set an example for society. Since the outbreak of the Japanese invasion, your association has even issued a general order prohibiting your members from representing those who undermine the patriotic movement and are convicted as traitors. Your patriotic zeal is deeply appreciated. Zhang Yaozeng and others, as lawyers in this city, should arouse their conscience and strictly comply with the resolution of your association. However, they openly and brazenly represented the traitor You in court, not only violating the resolution of your association but also abetting the evildoer and indirectly undermining the patriotic movement. They have completely lost their conscience. How can they have a conscience? At this critical moment of resisting Japan and saving the nation, we cannot tolerate such scum surviving in the world. Therefore, we send this letter to your association, urging you to uphold the spirit of your previous resolution and immediately warn Zhang Yaozeng and others to voluntarily terminate their contract to represent You in court and to severely punish Zhang Yaozeng and others to serve as a warning to others and to eliminate the scum. We also hope to receive a reply soon to affirm our public friendship.

To Be Handed Over to Su Zhenhui and Others Tomorrow

The Disaster Relief Office in this city was originally scheduled to close at the end of this month, and the disaster victims who came to Shanghai were also planned to be sent back by the end of this month. Also, Mr. Wang Yiting went to the office yesterday to discuss everything with Director Feng.
